LHAG TZAM GYI BAR CHUL SGRUB MCHOD KYI PHYAG LEN RNAMS BRJED

RGYA GAR NAS KROshA AU DA YA ZHES PA'I PAndI TA ZHIG 'ONGS PA'I
GNAS CHEN GYIS MCHOD SBYIN GYI RIL BUR BSGRUBS PA DANG, BYANG
CHUB SHING GI LO MA BYIN ZHING LEGS SBYAR GYI SKAD LAS

DRANGS PA'I BSNGAGS BRJOD SMON LAM BRTZAMS PA 'DAR BA LO TZ'A SA
BSGYUR BA NI, MING LDAN THAMS CAD SKYONG BA'I DPAL MNGA' MTHA'
KLAS YON TAN TSOGS KYIS BRGYAN BYAS SA YI ZLA BA STE, ,RIG DANG
YE SHES RGYA MTSOS YONGS GANG DPAL DANG LDAN

PA'I DGA' BA LA 'JUG LHA MIS MCHOD BYAD CING, ,CHA SHAS YONGS
RDZOGS DA DAG YAS SKYI 'GRO'I SDUG BSNGAL MA LUS LAGS BCOMS YANG
DAG DON LA 'GOD MDZAD PA, ,LHA LDAN GNAS SU THAMS CAD MKHYEN
KHYED BYE BA PHRAG BRGYAR BZHUGS GSOL

BDAG CAG RAB TU DANG BAS 'DUNG, ,KUN MKHYEN NYID DANG MES PO
TSANGS PA GNYIS, ,MTHA' YAS YON TAN SRANG LA GZHAL BA NA, ,BYED
PO YANG BAS MTHO RIS GNAS SU SONG, ,MGON KHYOD KYI LCI BAS SA
STENG GNAS ZHES GLENG, ,ZHES CHIG SBYOR

PHUN SUM TSOGS PA ZHIG SNANG NGO,, RTZAM 'THOR 'DI LA THAMS CAD
DGA' BA 'DUG PAS GSER SOGS KYI STER CHA LEGS PA BYAS, DGA' LDAN
GSUNG RAB GLING PA DANG DGA' LDAN DON GNYIS GLING PA GNYIS LA
SMAN BLA'I MDO CHOG, BZANG SPYOD,

@159B BYAMS SMON, SGROL MA, SHER SNYING, TSE GZUNGS RNAMS KYI
LUNG PHUL, GSUNG RAB GLING PA TSE'I TSIGS BCAD GSAR BA DE LAM RU
'DZIN LONG MA BYUNG BAS 'DI NYIN GDANGS 'UR GYI ZHAL 'DON MDZAD,
CHOS NYI SHU LAS SKYONG RGYA RI BA

YAB SRAS 'KHOR BCAS, DE MO DPON BO CAN LA GRUB RGYAL LUGS KYI LHA
GCIG BUM GCIG LA BSTEN PA'I TSE DBANG, SHANGS LUGS KYI RTA MGRAN
DANG PHYAG DRUG PA'I DBANG BZHI BYIN RLABS KYI TSUL DU BSKUR BA,
RNAM 'JOMS LJANG SNGON,

SGROL DKAR YID BZHIN 'KHOR LO, SME BRTZEGS DUD KHA RNAMS KYI RJES
GNANG PHUL, BDOG PA'I SKYES LAN DANG BCAS KHONG DPON G-YOG RANG
GNAS SU BYON, NYER GNYIS LA RTA TSAG SPRUL PA'I SKU, RVA SGRENG
MKHAN ZUR PA BSTAN PA DAR RGYAS,

'BRAS SPUNGS KYI SLOB DPON 'DRUG, MANYDZU SHR'I SKU SKYE, KHAL
KHA TSO BA BDUN GYI MI SNA DANG BCAS PA, 'DAR NAS BSOD NAMS LHUN
GRUB RDO RJE SGER GZHIS NAS 'ONGS BA LA JA GRAL BTANG, 'JAM
DBYANGS SPRUL SKU DANG THU SHI YE THU RGYAL POS GTZOS

PA LA KHING DPON KHAG TSO DANG SPYI PA'I YI GE RTEN BCAS SPRAD
CING NGAG MA ZHIB PAR GLENG, NYIN GSUM GYI BAR LA DGE TSUL DRUG
BRGYA DRUG CU RE GCIG DANG DGE SLANG SUM BRGYA LNGA BSGRUBS, NYER
DGU LA KHAL KHA'I MI SNA TSOR THUGS RJE CHEN PO GTZO

'KHOR GSUM BA'I RJES GNANG DANG SO SO'I YIG LAN RTEN SBRAGS NGAG
MA DANG BCAS RDZONG DANG 'BYAS, RGYAL PO'I GCUNG SIDDNYI SHR'I
HUNG THA'I JIS SKU GSUNG THUGS GSUM GYI BSTOD PA DGOS TSUL MDZAD
PA LTAR LUS NGAG YID GSUM YOD PA RGYA

KHO RANG GI JE JO DANG TSA BO DGRAR LANGS TE MNGA' THANG DANG
BRAL BAS NYAM THAG CI BA
